#покушение на главу НКР
country_event = {
	id = arme.2
	title = arme.2.t
	desc = arme.2.d
	picture = GFX_Pokuscenie_nkr_2000
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arme.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.2.a executed"
		trigger = {
			tag = ARM
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = arme.2.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.2.b executed"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = ARM
				tag = NKR
				tag = AZE
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = arme.2.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.2.c executed"
		trigger = {
			tag = NKR
		}
		add_political_power = -50
	}
	option = {
		name = arme.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.2.o1 executed"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = AZE
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = arme.3
	title = arme.3.t
	desc = arme.3.d
	picture = GFX_redbridge
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arme.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.3.a executed"
		trigger = {
			tag = ARM
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_to_variable = { party_pop_array^4 = 0.05 }
			recalculate_party = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = FRA_communist_rise_5_TT
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = arme.3.c
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.3.c executed"
		trigger = {
			tag = AZE
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
	}
}

		ARM = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = fossil_powerplant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -7.5 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { int_investment_change = 7.5 }
		modify_international_investment_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ARM }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		ARM = {
			country_event = arme.7
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = ARM
					value > 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = arme.15
	title = arme.15.t
	desc = arme.15.d
	picture = GFX_debates_arm
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arme.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.15.a executed"
		set_country_flag = oppos_lived
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ARM_echoes_1999_pac
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ARM_echoes_1999_pac
				add_idea = ARM_echoes_1999
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ARM_echoes_1999
			}
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 16 }
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_popularity_increase = 0.1
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_outlook_increase = 0.1
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_index = 19 }
			set_temp_variable = {
				party_popularity_increase = 0.1
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				temp_outlook_increase = 0.1
			}
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = ARM_echoes_1999_pac
					has_idea = ARM_echoes_1999
				}
			}
			add_ideas = ARM_echoes_1999
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = arme.16
	title = arme.16.t
	desc = arme.16.d
	picture = GFX_ukr_cis
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arme.16.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.16.a executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		add_command_power = 10
		army_experience = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = sunni
			}
			set_temp_variable = { rad_change = -5 }
			modify_radicalization_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					original_tag = ARM
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ARM }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { modify_eurosceptic_target = ARM }
		eurosceptic_change = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = recent_actions_positive
			target = GRE
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = recent_actions_positive
			target = GRE
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ARM modifier = supports_us }
		}
	}
}

	desc = arme.122.d
	picture = GFX_arm_usa_relationship
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arme.122.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arme.122.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ARM_national_guard_idea
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ARM_national_guard_idea
				add_idea = ARM_national_guard_idea1
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ARM_inner_army_idea
			add_idea = ARM_inner_army_idea1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = recent_actions_positive }
	}
}

###Levon Petrosyan
country_event = {
	id = arm_levon.1
	title = arm_levon.1.t
	desc = arm_levon.1.d
	picture = GFX_arm_tur_prot_ev
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arm_levon.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arm_levon.1.a executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARM = {
					has_idea = ARM_crossroad_diplomacy_idea
				}
			}
			ARM = {
				country_event = arm_levon.2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARM = {
					has_idea = ARM_crossroad_diplomacy_idea_1
				}
			}
			ARM = {
				country_event = arm_levon.3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARM = {
					has_idea = ARM_crossroad_diplomacy_idea_2
				}
			}
			ARM = {
				country_event = arm_levon.4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ARM = {
					has_idea = ARM_crossroad_diplomacy_idea_3
				}

	desc = arm_foreign_legion.3.d
	picture = GFX_arm_foreign_legion
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = arm_foreign_legion.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arm_foreign_legion.3.a executed"
		add_ideas = ARM_armenian_foreign_legion_moblize_idea
		ARM = {
			country_event = arm_foreign_legion.4
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ARM }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Foreign Legion Brigade"
				is_locked = yes
				regiments = {
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					L_Recce_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } }
				prioritize = { 1140 }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"[Armenia] Foreign Legion Brigade\" division_template = \"Foreign Legion Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ARM
					value > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = arm_foreign_legion.3.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: arm_foreign_legion.3.b executed"
		ARM = {
			country_event = arm_foreign_legion.5
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_opinion = {
					target = ARM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}

	}
}

					division = "name = \"Western Armenian Battalion\" division_template = \"Western Armenian Battalion\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		add_autonomy_score = { value = -700 }
		ARM = {
			remove_ideas = ARM_turkey_compliance_idea
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ROOT
				autonomous_state = autonomy_autonomous_state
				end_wars = no
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
		}
	}

					has_government = nationalist
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
	}
